All notable changes to this project will be documented in this file.

The format is based on \href{https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.0.0/}{\texttt{ Keep a Changelog}}, and this project adheres to \href{https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html}{\texttt{ Semantic Versioning}}.\hypertarget{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{Unreleased}{Unreleased}}\label{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1}
\hypertarget{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{5.\+10.\+0 -\/ 2021-\/10-\/11}{5.\+10.\+0 -\/ 2021-\/10-\/11}}\label{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md2}
\hypertarget{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md3}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md3}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added a new {\ttfamily URI.\+is\+Dom\+Safe(uri)} \doxylink{class_a_p_i}{API} to check if a URI is considered safe to be inserted into the DOM \#\+TINY-\/7998
\item Added the {\ttfamily ESC} key code constant to the {\ttfamily VK} \doxylink{class_a_p_i}{API} \#\+TINY-\/7917
\item Added a new {\ttfamily deprecation\+\_\+warnings} setting for turning off deprecation console warning messages \#\+TINY-\/8049
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md4}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Improved}{Improved}}\label{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md4}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily element} argument of the {\ttfamily editor.\+selection.\+scroll\+Into\+View()} \doxylink{class_a_p_i}{API} is now optional, and if it is not provided the current selection will be scrolled into view \#\+TINY-\/7291
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md5}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md5}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The deprecated {\ttfamily scope} attribute is no longer added to {\ttfamily td} cells when converting a row to a header row \#\+TINY-\/7731
\item The number of {\ttfamily col} elements is normalized to match the number of columns in a table after a table action \#\+TINY-\/8011
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md6}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md6}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed a regression that caused block wrapper formats to apply and remove incorrectly when using a collapsed selection with multiple words \#\+TINY-\/8036
\item Resizing table columns in some scenarios would resize the column to an incorrect position \#\+TINY-\/7731
\item Inserting a table where the parent element had padding would cause the table width to be incorrect \#\+TINY-\/7991
\item The resize backdrop element did not have the {\ttfamily data-\/mce-\/bogus="{}all"{}} attribute set to prevent it being included in output \#\+TINY-\/7854
\item Resize handles appeared on top of dialogs and menus when using an inline editor \#\+TINY-\/3263
\item Fixed the {\ttfamily autoresize} plugin incorrectly scrolling to the top of the editor content in some cases when changing content \#\+TINY-\/7291
\item Fixed the {\ttfamily editor.\+selection.\+scroll\+Into\+View()} type signature, as it incorrectly required an {\ttfamily Element} instead of {\ttfamily HTMLElement} \#\+TINY-\/7291
\item Table cells that were both row and column headers did not retain the correct state when converting back to a regular row or column \#\+TINY-\/7709
\item Clicking beside a non-\/editable element could cause the editor to incorrectly scroll to the top of the content \#\+TINY-\/7062
\item Clicking in a table cell, with a non-\/editable element in an adjacent cell, incorrectly caused the non-\/editable element to be selected \#\+TINY-\/7736
\item Split toolbar buttons incorrectly had nested {\ttfamily tabindex="{}-\/1"{}} attributes \#\+TINY-\/7879
\item Fixed notifications rendering in the wrong place initially and when the page was scrolled \#\+TINY-\/7894
\item Fixed an exception getting thrown when the number of {\ttfamily col} elements didn\textquotesingle{}t match the number of columns in a table \#\+TINY-\/7041 \#\+TINY-\/8011
\item The table selection state could become incorrect after selecting a noneditable table cell \#\+TINY-\/8053
\item As of Mozilla Firefox 91, toggling fullscreen mode with {\ttfamily toolbar\+\_\+sticky} enabled would cause the toolbar to disappear \#\+TINY-\/7873
\item Fixed URLs not cleaned correctly in some cases in the {\ttfamily link} and {\ttfamily image} plugins \#\+TINY-\/7998
\item Fixed the {\ttfamily image} and {\ttfamily media} toolbar buttons incorrectly appearing to be in an inactive state in some cases \#\+TINY-\/3463
\item Fixed the {\ttfamily editor.\+selection.\+selector\+Changed} \doxylink{class_a_p_i}{API} not firing if the selector matched the current selection when registered in some cases \#\+TINY-\/3463
\item Inserting content into a {\ttfamily contenteditable="{}true"{}} element that was contained within a {\ttfamily contenteditable="{}false"{}} element would move the selection to an incorrect location \#\+TINY-\/7842
\item Dragging and dropping {\ttfamily contenteditable="{}false"{}} elements could result in the element being placed in an unexpected location \#\+TINY-\/7917
\item Pressing the Escape key would not cancel a drag action that started on a {\ttfamily contenteditable="{}false"{}} element within the editor \#\+TINY-\/7917
\item {\ttfamily video} and {\ttfamily audio} elements were unable to be played when the {\ttfamily media} plugin live embeds were enabled in some cases \#\+TINY-\/7674
\item Pasting images would throw an exception if the clipboard {\ttfamily items} were not files (for example, screenshots taken from gnome-\/software). Patch contributed by cedric-\/anne \#\+TINY-\/8079
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md7}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Deprecated}{Deprecated}}\label{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md7}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Several APIs have been deprecated. See the release notes section for information \#\+TINY-\/8023 \#\+TINY-\/8063
\item Several Editor settings have been deprecated. See the release notes section for information \#\+TINY-\/8086
\item The Table of Contents and Image Tools plugins will be classified as Premium plugins in the next major release \#\+TINY-\/8087
\item Word support in the {\ttfamily paste} plugin has been deprecated and will be removed in the next major release \#\+TINY-\/8087
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md8}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{5.\+9.\+2 -\/ 2021-\/09-\/08}{5.\+9.\+2 -\/ 2021-\/09-\/08}}\label{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md8}
\hypertarget{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md9}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md9}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed an exception getting thrown when disabling events and setting content \#\+TINY-\/7956
\item Delete operations could behave incorrectly if the selection crossed a table boundary \#\+TINY-\/7596
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md10}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{5.\+9.\+1 -\/ 2021-\/08-\/27}{5.\+9.\+1 -\/ 2021-\/08-\/27}}\label{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md10}
\hypertarget{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md11}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md11}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Published Tiny\+MCE types failed to compile in strict mode \#\+TINY-\/7915
\item The {\ttfamily Table\+Modified} event sometimes didn\textquotesingle{}t fire when performing certain table actions \#\+TINY-\/7916
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md12}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{5.\+9.\+0 -\/ 2021-\/08-\/26}{5.\+9.\+0 -\/ 2021-\/08-\/26}}\label{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md12}
\hypertarget{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md13}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md13}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added a new {\ttfamily mce\+Focus} command that focuses the editor. Equivalent to using {\ttfamily editor.\+focus()} \#\+TINY-\/7373
\item Added a new {\ttfamily mce\+Table\+Toggle\+Class} command which toggles the provided class on the currently selected table \#\+TINY-\/7476
\item Added a new {\ttfamily mce\+Table\+Cell\+Toggle\+Class} command which toggles the provided class on the currently selected table cells \#\+TINY-\/7476
\item Added a new {\ttfamily tablecellvalign} toolbar button and menu item for vertical table cell alignment \#\+TINY-\/7477
\item Added a new {\ttfamily tablecellborderwidth} toolbar button and menu item to change table cell border width \#\+TINY-\/7478
\item Added a new {\ttfamily tablecellborderstyle} toolbar button and menu item to change table cell border style \#\+TINY-\/7478
\item Added a new {\ttfamily tablecaption} toolbar button and menu item to toggle captions on tables \#\+TINY-\/7479
\item Added a new {\ttfamily mce\+Table\+Toggle\+Caption} command that toggles captions on a selected table \#\+TINY-\/7479
\item Added a new {\ttfamily tablerowheader} toolbar button and menu item to toggle the header state of row cells \#\+TINY-\/7478
\item Added a new {\ttfamily tablecolheader} toolbar button and menu item to toggle the header state of column cells \#\+TINY-\/7482
\item Added a new {\ttfamily tablecellbordercolor} toolbar button and menu item to select table cell border colors, with an accompanying setting {\ttfamily table\+\_\+border\+\_\+color\+\_\+map} to customize the available values \#\+TINY-\/7480
\item Added a new {\ttfamily tablecellbackgroundcolor} toolbar button and menu item to select table cell background colors, with an accompanying setting {\ttfamily table\+\_\+background\+\_\+color\+\_\+map} to customize the available values \#\+TINY-\/7480
\item Added a new {\ttfamily language} menu item and toolbar button to add {\ttfamily lang} attributes to content, with an accompanying {\ttfamily content\+\_\+langs} setting to specify the languages available \#\+TINY-\/6149
\item A new {\ttfamily lang} format is now available that can be used with {\ttfamily editor.\+formatter}, or applied with the {\ttfamily Lang} editor command \#\+TINY-\/6149
\item Added a new {\ttfamily language} icon for the {\ttfamily language} toolbar button \#\+TINY-\/7670
\item Added a new {\ttfamily table-\/row-\/numbering} icon \#\+TINY-\/7327
\item Added new plugin commands\+: {\ttfamily mce\+Emoticons} (Emoticons), {\ttfamily mce\+Word\+Count} (Word Count), and {\ttfamily mce\+Template} (\doxylink{class_template}{Template}) \#\+TINY-\/7619
\item Added a new {\ttfamily iframe\+\_\+aria\+\_\+text} setting to set the iframe title attribute \#\+TINY-\/1264
\item Added a new Dom\+Parser {\ttfamily Node.\+children()} \doxylink{class_a_p_i}{API} to return all the children of a {\ttfamily Node} \#\+TINY-\/7756
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md14}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Improved}{Improved}}\label{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md14}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Sticky toolbars can now be offset from the top of the page using the new {\ttfamily toolbar\+\_\+sticky\+\_\+offset} setting \#\+TINY-\/7337
\item Fancy menu items now accept an {\ttfamily init\+Data} property to allow custom initialization data \#\+TINY-\/7480
\item Improved the load time of the {\ttfamily fullpage} plugin by using the existing editor schema rather than creating a new one \#\+TINY-\/6504
\item Improved the performance when UI components are rendered \#\+TINY-\/7572
\item The context toolbar no longer unnecessarily repositions to the top of large elements when scrolling \#\+TINY-\/7545
\item The context toolbar will now move out of the way when it overlaps with the selection, such as in table cells \#\+TINY-\/7192
\item The context toolbar now uses a short animation when transitioning between different locations \#\+TINY-\/7740
\item {\ttfamily Env.\+browser} now uses the User-\/\+Agent Client Hints \doxylink{class_a_p_i}{API} where it is available \#\+TINY-\/7785
\item Icons with a {\ttfamily -\/rtl} suffix in their name will now automatically be used when the UI is rendered in right-\/to-\/left mode \#\+TINY-\/7782
\item The {\ttfamily formatter.\+match} \doxylink{class_a_p_i}{API} now accepts an optional {\ttfamily similar} parameter to check if the format partially matches \#\+TINY-\/7712
\item The {\ttfamily formatter.\+format\+Changed} \doxylink{class_a_p_i}{API} now supports providing format variables when listening for changes \#\+TINY-\/7713
\item The formatter will now fire {\ttfamily Format\+Apply} and {\ttfamily Format\+Remove} events for the relevant actions \#\+TINY-\/7713
\item The {\ttfamily autolink} plugin link detection now permits custom protocols \#\+TINY-\/7714
\item The {\ttfamily autolink} plugin valid link detection has been improved \#\+TINY-\/7714
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md15}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Changed}{Changed}}\label{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md15}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Changed the load order so content CSS is loaded before the editor is populated with content \#\+TINY-\/7249
\item Changed the {\ttfamily emoticons}, {\ttfamily wordcount}, {\ttfamily code}, {\ttfamily codesample}, and {\ttfamily template} plugins to open dialogs using commands \#\+TINY-\/7619
\item The context toolbar will no longer show an arrow when it overlaps the content, such as in table cells \#\+TINY-\/7665
\item The context toolbar will no longer overlap the statusbar for toolbars using {\ttfamily node} or {\ttfamily selection} positions \#\+TINY-\/7666
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md16}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md16}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily editor.\+fire} \doxylink{class_a_p_i}{API} was incorrectly mutating the original {\ttfamily args} provided \#\+TINY-\/3254
\item Unbinding an event handler did not take effect immediately while the event was firing \#\+TINY-\/7436
\item Binding an event handler incorrectly took effect immediately while the event was firing \#\+TINY-\/7436
\item Unbinding a native event handler inside the {\ttfamily remove} event caused an exception that blocked editor removal \#\+TINY-\/7730
\item The {\ttfamily Set\+Content} event contained the incorrect {\ttfamily content} when using the {\ttfamily editor.\+selection.\+set\+Content()} \doxylink{class_a_p_i}{API} \#\+TINY-\/3254
\item The editor content could be edited after calling {\ttfamily set\+Progress\+State(true)} in iframe mode \#\+TINY-\/7373
\item Tabbing out of the editor after calling {\ttfamily set\+Progress\+State(true)} behaved inconsistently in iframe mode \#\+TINY-\/7373
\item Flash of unstyled content while loading the editor because the content CSS was loaded after the editor content was rendered \#\+TINY-\/7249
\item Partially transparent RGBA values provided in the {\ttfamily color\+\_\+map} setting were given the wrong hex value \#\+TINY-\/7163
\item HTML comments with mismatched quotes were parsed incorrectly under certain circumstances \#\+TINY-\/7589
\item The editor could crash when inserting certain HTML content \#\+TINY-\/7756
\item Inserting certain HTML content into the editor could result in invalid HTML once parsed \#\+TINY-\/7756
\item Links in notification text did not show the correct mouse pointer \#\+TINY-\/7661
\item Using the Tab key to navigate into the editor on Microsoft Internet Explorer 11 would incorrectly focus the toolbar \#\+TINY-\/3707
\item The editor selection could be placed in an incorrect location when undoing or redoing changes in a document containing {\ttfamily contenteditable="{}false"{}} elements \#\+TINY-\/7663
\item Menus and context menus were not closed when clicking into a different editor \#\+TINY-\/7399
\item Context menus on Android were not displayed when more than one HTML element was selected \#\+TINY-\/7688
\item Disabled nested menu items could still be opened \#\+TINY-\/7700
\item The nested menu item chevron icon was not fading when the menu item was disabled \#\+TINY-\/7700
\item {\ttfamily imagetools} buttons were incorrectly enabled for remote images without {\ttfamily imagetools\+\_\+proxy} set \#\+TINY-\/7772
\item Only table content would be deleted when partially selecting a table and content outside the table \#\+TINY-\/6044
\item The table cell selection handling was incorrect in some cases when dealing with nested tables \#\+TINY-\/6298
\item Removing a table row or column could result in the cursor getting placed in an invalid location \#\+TINY-\/7695
\item Pressing the Tab key to navigate through table cells did not skip noneditable cells \#\+TINY-\/7705
\item Clicking on a noneditable table cell did not show a visual selection like other noneditable elements \#\+TINY-\/7724
\item Some table operations would incorrectly cause table row attributes and styles to be lost \#\+TINY-\/6666
\item The selection was incorrectly lost when using the {\ttfamily mce\+Table\+Cell\+Type} and {\ttfamily mce\+Table\+Row\+Type} commands \#\+TINY-\/6666
\item The {\ttfamily mce\+Table\+Row\+Type} was reversing the order of the rows when converting multiple header rows back to body rows \#\+TINY-\/6666
\item The table dialog did not always respect the {\ttfamily table\+\_\+style\+\_\+with\+\_\+css} option \#\+TINY-\/4926
\item Pasting into a table with multiple cells selected could cause the content to be pasted in the wrong location \#\+TINY-\/7485
\item The {\ttfamily Table\+Modified} event was not fired when pasting cells into a table \#\+TINY-\/6939
\item The table paste column before and after icons were not flipped in RTL mode \#\+TINY-\/7851
\item Fixed table corruption when deleting a {\ttfamily contenteditable="{}false"{}} cell \#\+TINY-\/7891
\item The {\ttfamily dir} attribute was being incorrectly applied to list items \#\+TINY-\/4589
\item Applying selector formats would sometimes not apply the format correctly to elements in a list \#\+TINY-\/7393
\item For formats that specify an attribute or style that should be removed, the formatter {\ttfamily match} \doxylink{class_a_p_i}{API} incorrectly returned {\ttfamily false} \#\+TINY-\/6149
\item The type signature on the {\ttfamily formatter.\+match\+Node} \doxylink{class_a_p_i}{API} had the wrong return type (was {\ttfamily boolean} but should have been {\ttfamily Formatter \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} undefined}) \#\+TINY-\/6149
\item The {\ttfamily formatter.\+format\+Changed} \doxylink{class_a_p_i}{API} would ignore the {\ttfamily similar} parameter if another callback had already been registered for the same format \#\+TINY-\/7713
\item The {\ttfamily formatter.\+format\+Changed} \doxylink{class_a_p_i}{API} would sometimes not run the callback the first time the format was removed \#\+TINY-\/7713
\item Base64 encoded images with spaces or line breaks in the data URI were not displayed correctly. Patch contributed by Robo\+Burned
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md17}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Deprecated}{Deprecated}}\label{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md17}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily bbcode}, {\ttfamily fullpage}, {\ttfamily legacyoutput}, and {\ttfamily spellchecker} plugins have been deprecated and marked for removal in the next major release \#\+TINY-\/7260

\item Fixed an issue when pasting cells from tables containing {\ttfamily colgroup}s into tables without {\ttfamily colgroup}s \#\+TINY-\/6675
\item Fixed an issue that could cause an invalid toolbar button state when multiple inline editors were on a single page \#\+TINY-\/6297

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item An unexpected exception was thrown when switching to readonly mode and adjusting the editor width \#\+TINY-\/6383
\item Content could be lost when the {\ttfamily pagebreak\+\_\+split\+\_\+block} setting was enabled \#\+TINY-\/3388
\item The {\ttfamily list-\/style-\/type\+: none;} style on nested list items was incorrectly removed when clearing formatting \#\+TINY-\/6264

\item Properties on the {\ttfamily Open\+Notification} event were incorrectly namespaced \#\+TINY-\/7486

\hypertarget{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md23}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md23}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added the {\ttfamily PAGE\+\_\+\+UP} and {\ttfamily PAGE\+\_\+\+DOWN} key code constants to the {\ttfamily VK} \doxylink{class_a_p_i}{API} \#\+TINY-\/4612
\item The editor resize handle can now be controlled using the keyboard \#\+TINY-\/4823
\item Added a new {\ttfamily fixed\+\_\+toolbar\+\_\+container\+\_\+target} setting which renders the toolbar in the specified {\ttfamily HTMLElement}. Patch contributed by pvrobays

\begin{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added new table\+\_\+resize\+\_\+bars configuration setting. This setting allows you to disable the table resize bars.
\item Added new before\+Initialize event to tinymce.\+util.\+XHR lets you modify XHR properties before open. Patch contributed by Brent Clintel.
\item Added new autolink\+\_\+pattern setting to autolink plugin. Enables you to override the default autolink formats. Patch contributed by Ben Tiedt.
\item Added new charmap option that lets you override the default charmap of the charmap plugin.
\item Added new charmap\+\_\+append option that lets you add new characters to the default charmap of the charmap plugin.
\item Added new insert\+Custom\+Char event that gets fired when a character is inserted by the charmap plugin.

\item Added new live previews of embeded videos. Lets you play the video right inside the editor.
\item Added new set\+Dirty method and "{}dirty"{} event to the editor. Makes it easier to track the dirty state change.
\item Added new set\+Mode method to Editor instances that lets you dynamically switch between design/readonly.
\item Added new core support for content\+Editable=false elements within the editor overrides the browsers broken behavior.

\item Fixed so inline mode toolbar gets rendered right aligned if the editable element positioned to the documents right edge.
\item Fixed so empty inline elements inside empty block elements doesn\textquotesingle{}t get removed if configured to be kept intact.
\item Fixed so Dom\+Query parents\+Until/prev\+Until/next\+Until supports selectors/elements/filters etc.
\item Fixed so legacyoutput plugin overrides fontselect and fontsizeselect controls and handles font elements properly.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md390}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{4.\+1.\+0 -\/ 2014-\/06-\/18}{4.\+1.\+0 -\/ 2014-\/06-\/18}}\label{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md390}
\hypertarget{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md391}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Added}{Added}}\label{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md391}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Added new file\+\_\+picker\+\_\+callback option to replace the old file\+\_\+browser\+\_\+callback the latter will still work though.
\item Added new custom colors to textcolor plugin will be displayed if a color picker is provided also shows the latest colors.
\item Added new color\+\_\+picker\+\_\+callback option to enable you to add custom color pickers to the editor.
\item Added new advanced tabs to table/cell/row dialogs to enable you to select colors for border/background.
\item Added new colorpicker plugin that lets you select colors from a hsv color picker.
\item Added new tinymce.\+util.\+Color class to handle color parsing and converting.
\item Added new colorpicker UI widget element lets you add a hsv color picker to any form/window.
\item Added new textpattern plugin that allows you to use markdown like text patterns to format contents.
\item Added new resize helper element that shows the current width \& height while resizing.
\item Added new "{}once"{} method to Editor and Event\+Dispatcher enables since callback execution events.
\item Added new j\+Query like class under tinymce.\+dom.\+Dom\+Query it\textquotesingle{}s exposed on editor instances (editor.\$) and globally under (tinymce.\$).
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md392}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Fixed}{Fixed}}\label{md_assets_2vendors_2tinymce_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md392}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Fixed so the default resize method for images are proportional shift/ctrl can be used to make an unproportional size.
\item Fixed bug where the image\+\_\+dimensions option of the image plugin would cause exceptions when it tried to update the size.
\item Fixed bug where table cell dialog class field wasn\textquotesingle{}t properly updated when editing an a table cell with an existing class.
\item Fixed bug where Safari on Mac would produce webkit-\/fake-\/url for pasted images so these are now removed.
\item Fixed bug where the node\+Change event would get fired before the selection was changed when clicking inside the current selection range.
\item Fixed bug where valid\+\_\+classes option would cause exception when it removed internal prefixed classes like mce-\/item-\/.
\item Fixed bug where backspace would cause navigation in IE 8 on an inline element and after a caret formatting was applied.
\item Fixed so placeholder images produced by the media plugin gets selected when inserted/edited.
\item Fixed so it\textquotesingle{}s possible to drag in images when the paste\+\_\+data\+\_\+images option is enabled. Might be useful for mail clients.
\item Fixed so images doesn\textquotesingle{}t get a width/height applied if the image\+\_\+dimensions option is set to false useful for responsive contents.
\item Fixed so it\textquotesingle{}s possible to pass in an optional arguments object for the node\+Changed function to be passed to all nodechange event listeners.
\item Fixed bug where media plugin embed code didn\textquotesingle{}t update correctly. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
